if (TransMenu.isSupported()) {
TransMenu.initialize();

 menu310.ondeactivate = function() {document.getElementById("menu310").className = ""; };
 menu329.onactivate = function() {document.getElementById("menu329").className = "hover"; };
 menu329.ondeactivate = function() {document.getElementById("menu329").className = ""; };

 menu311.ondeactivate = function() {document.getElementById("menu311").className = ""; };
 menu305.onactivate = function() {document.getElementById("menu305").className = "hover"; };
 menu305.ondeactivate = function() {document.getElementById("menu305").className = ""; };
 document.getElementById("menu307").onmouseover = function() {
ms.hideCurrent();
this.className = "hover";
}
document.getElementById("menu307").onmouseout = function() { this.className = ""; }
}}

else if ( typeof window.attachEvent != "undefined" ) {
window.attachEvent( "onload", init);
}else{
if ( window.onload != null ) {
var oldOnload = window.onload;
window.onload = function ( e ) {
oldOnload( e );
init();
}
}else
window.onload = init();
}

          function left_search_clear(el) {
	if (el.value == "Search" ||
	el.value == "Search"
	) {
		el.value = "";
		//W2U SEF URL
                document.forms.left_search_form.action = "http://www.weather2umbrella.com/en/weather-forecast-search-results/"+"eta2/10/";
		
	}
}

function left_search_blur(el) {
	if (!left_getElementByClass('left_suggest_link_over')) {
		document.getElementById('left_search_suggest').style.visibility="hidden";
		if (el.value == "") {
			el.value = "Search";
		}
	}
}

var city_link = "http://www.weather2umbrella.com/index.php?option=com_content&amp;view=article&amp;id=93";
var country_link = "http://www.weather2umbrella.com/index.php?option=com_content&amp;view=article&amp;id=94";
var region_link = "http://www.weather2umbrella.com/index.php?option=com_content&amp;view=article&amp;id=95";
var search_result_link = "http://www.weather2umbrella.com/index.php?option=com_content&amp;view=article&amp;id=307";

//Click (za search suggest)
function left_setSearch(value) {
	// Opera fix
	if (BrowserDetect.browser == "Opera") {
		var search_val = value.split("&gt;");
		search_val2 = search_val[1].split("&lt;");
		key_field = document.getElementById('left_search_keyword');
		key_field.value = search_val2[0].replace(/^\s\s*/, '').replace(/\s\s*$/, '');
	} else {
		var search_val = value.split(/\&amp;nbsp\;/gi);
		search_val2 = search_val[1].split(/\&lt;\/span\&gt;/gi);
		key_field = document.getElementById('left_search_keyword');
		key_field.value = search_val2[0].replace(/^\s\s*/, '').replace(/\s\s*$/, '');
		search_val3 = search_val2[1].split(/\&gt;/gi);
	}

	region_field = document.getElementById('left_region_name');
	country_field = document.getElementById('left_country_name');
	
	var search_val4 = "";

	// Opera fix
	if (BrowserDetect.browser == "Opera")
		search_val4 = search_val[3].split("&lt;");
	else
	if (search_val3[1])
		search_val4 = search_val3[1].split(/\&lt;span\&gt;/gi);

	if (search_val4[0]) {
		region_field.value = search_val4[0].replace(/^\s\s*/, '').replace(/\s\s*$/, '');
		country_field.value = search_val4[0].replace(/^\s\s*/, '').replace(/\s\s*$/, '');
	}
	sugg_field = document.getElementById('left_search_suggest');
	sugg_field.innerHTML = '';
	sugg_field.style.visibility="hidden";
	key_field.focus();
	
		var cityid = "";

                // Opera fix
                if (BrowserDetect.browser == "Opera")
                        cityid = search_val[4].split("cid");
                else
                if (search_val2[2])
                        cityid = search_val2[2].split(/cid/gi);

                var city_id = "";
                if (cityid[1])
                        city_id = cityid[1].substr(1, cityid[1].length-2);
                if (city_id)
                        document.getElementById('left_city_id').value = city_id;


	var test_str = search_val[0].substr(0, 56);
	if (test_str == '&lt;span class="left_suggest_keyword" style="color: #5e8513' ||
	    test_str == '&lt;SPAN class="left_suggest_keyword" style="color: #5e8513' ||
	    test_str == '&lt;span class="left_suggest_keyword" style="color: rgb(94,' ||
	    test_str == '&lt;SPAN style="COLOR: #5e8513" class=left_suggest_keyword&gt;') {
		region_field.value = key_field.value;
		country_field.value = '';
		document.forms.left_search_form.action = region_link;

		//W2U SEF URL
		document.forms.left_search_form.action = "http://www.weather2umbrella.com/en/weather-forecast-"+key_field.value.replace(/ /g, "-").toLowerCase()+"/"+"eta2/2/"+city_id+"/0";

		
	} else 
	if (test_str == '&lt;span class="left_suggest_keyword" style="color: #ff8400' ||
	    test_str == '&lt;SPAN class="left_suggest_keyword" style="color: #ff8400' ||
	    test_str == '&lt;span class="left_suggest_keyword" style="color: rgb(255' ||
            test_str == '&lt;SPAN style="COLOR: #ff8400" class=left_suggest_keyword&gt;') {
		country_field.value = key_field.value;
		document.forms.left_search_form.action = country_link;
		
		//w2U SEF URL	
		document.forms.left_search_form.action = "http://www.weather2umbrella.com/en/weather-forecast-"+key_field.value.replace(/ /g, "-").toLowerCase()+"/"+"eta2/3/"+city_id+"/0";


	} else {
		region_field.value = '';
		country_field.value = '';
		document.forms.left_search_form.action = city_link;

		//W2U SEF URL
		document.forms.left_search_form.action = "http://www.weather2umbrella.com/en/weather-forecast-"+key_field.value.replace(/ /g, "-").toLowerCase()+"/"+"eta2/1/"+city_id+"/0/3h";
	}
	
	left_submit_keyword();
	
}

function left_content_search_keydown(key_Code) {
        //alert(key_Code);
        if (key_Code==13){ // enter
                        left_submit_keyword();
        } else
        if (key_Code==40){ // down arrow
                left_content_search_change_focus(1, typed_search_val);
        } else
        if (key_Code==38){ // up arrow
                left_content_search_change_focus(-1, typed_search_val);
        }  else
        if (key_Code==27){ // up arrow
                document.getElementById('left_search_suggest').style.visibility="hidden";
                return;
        } else {
		//W2U SEF URL
                document.forms.left_search_form.action = "http://www.weather2umbrella.com/en/weather-forecast/"+"eta2/10/"+ document.getElementById('left_search_keyword').value.replace(/ /g, "-").toLowerCase() + String.fromCharCode(key_Code).toLowerCase();

        }
}

//submitovanje klujucne reci za pretrazivanje baze
function left_submit_keyword()
{
        keyword=document.getElementById('left_search_keyword').value;
        document.getElementById('left_searchword').value = keyword;

        document.getElementById('left_city_name').value = keyword;
	
        document.getElementById('left_search_form').submit();
}

function left_content_search_change_focus(delta, typed_search_val) {
	var new_selected_value = parseInt(left_getElementByClass('left_suggest_link_over'), 10);
	//alert(new_selected_value);
	if (isNaN(new_selected_value)) {
		if (delta == -1) {
			new_selected_value = num_results;
		} else {
			new_selected_value = -1;
		}
	}
	
	if (new_selected_value != -1 &amp;&amp; new_selected_value != num_results) {
		el_id = 'left_suggest_' + new_selected_value;
		
		document.getElementById(el_id).className = 'left_suggest_link';
	}
	
	new_selected_value = new_selected_value + delta;
	
	el_id = 'left_suggest_' + new_selected_value;
	
	el = document.getElementById(el_id);

	key_field = document.getElementById('left_search_keyword');

	if (!el) {
		//alert('YEA!');
		key_field.value = typed_search_val;
		document.forms.left_search_form.action = search_result_link;

		//W2U SEF URL
                document.forms.left_search_form.action = "http://www.weather2umbrella.com/en/weather-forecast/"+"eta2/10/"+ key_field.value.replace(/ /g, "-").toLowerCase();

	} else {
		
		el.className = 'left_suggest_link_over';
		value = el.innerHTML;

		if (BrowserDetect.browser == "Opera") {
	                var search_val = value.split("&gt;");
                	search_val2 = search_val[1].split("&lt;");
                	key_field = document.getElementById('left_search_keyword');
                	key_field.value = search_val2[0].replace(/^\s\s*/, '').replace(/\s\s*$/, '');
                	search_val4 = search_val[3].split("&lt;");
        	} else {
	                var search_val = value.split(/\&amp;nbsp\;/gi);
        	        search_val2 = search_val[1].split(/\&lt;\/span\&gt;/gi);
                	key_field = document.getElementById('left_search_keyword');
                	key_field.value = search_val2[0].replace(/^\s\s*/, '').replace(/\s\s*$/, '');
                	search_val3 = search_val2[1].split(/\&gt;/gi);
                	search_val4 = search_val3[1].split(/\&lt;span\&gt;/gi);
        	}
		

		country_field = document.getElementById('left_country_name');
		region_field = document.getElementById('left_region_name');

		country_field.value = search_val4[0].replace(/^\s\s*/, '').replace(/\s\s*$/, '');
	
			var cityid = "";

			if (BrowserDetect.browser == "Opera")
                        	cityid = search_val[4].split("cid");
                	else
		        if (search_val2[2])
                        	cityid = search_val2[2].split(/cid/gi);

			var city_id = "";
			if (cityid[1])
				city_id = cityid[1].substr(1, cityid[1].length-2);
			if (!city_id) city_id = "";
			document.getElementById('left_city_id').value = city_id;
	
		var test_str = search_val[0].substr(0, 56);
		//alert(test_str);
		if (test_str == '&lt;span class="left_suggest_keyword" style="color: #5e8513' ||
	    	    test_str == '&lt;SPAN class="left_suggest_keyword" style="color: #5e8513' ||
		    test_str == '&lt;span class="left_suggest_keyword" style="color: rgb(94,' ||
	      	    test_str == '&lt;SPAN style="COLOR: #5e8513" class=left_suggest_keyword&gt;') {
			//alert('REGION!');
			region_field.value = key_field.value;
			country_field.value = '';
			document.forms.left_search_form.action = region_link;

			//W2U SEF URL
	                document.forms.left_search_form.action = "http://www.weather2umbrella.com/en/weather-forecast-"+key_field.value.replace(/ /g, "-").toLowerCase()+"/"+"eta2/2/"+city_id+"/0";

		} else 
		if (test_str == '&lt;span class="left_suggest_keyword" style="color: #ff8400' ||
	    	    test_str == '&lt;SPAN class="left_suggest_keyword" style="color: #ff8400' ||
		    test_str == '&lt;span class="left_suggest_keyword" style="color: rgb(255' ||
                    test_str == '&lt;SPAN style="COLOR: #ff8400" class=left_suggest_keyword&gt;') {
			country_field.value = key_field.value;
			document.forms.left_search_form.action = country_link;

			//w2U SEF URL
	                document.forms.left_search_form.action = "http://www.weather2umbrella.com/en/weather-forecast-"+key_field.value.replace(/ /g, "-").toLowerCase()+"/"+"eta2/3/"+city_id+"/0";

		} else {
			region_field.value = '';
			country_field.value = '';
			document.forms.left_search_form.action = city_link;

			//W2U SEF URL
	                document.forms.left_search_form.action = "http://www.weather2umbrella.com/en/weather-forecast-"+key_field.value.replace(/ /g, "-").toLowerCase()+"/"+"eta2/1/"+city_id+"/0/3h";
		}
	}
}

function left_content_search(key_Code, table_name, table_key, table_fields, sort_field, sort_order, where_condition) {
	//alert(key_Code);
	if (!left_getElementByClass('left_suggest_link_over')) {
		typed_search_val = document.getElementById('left_search_keyword').value;
	}
	
	if (key_Code in set(37, 38, 39, 40,   27)){ // arrows + esc
		return false;
	}
	//alert(key_Code);

	var str = escape(typed_search_val.value);
	
	if (str === "") { //sluzi da sakrije div sa rezultatima ako ih nema
		document.getElementById('left_search_suggest').style.visibility="hidden";
		return;
	}
	
	var callback = function(responseText) {
		{
        		var decoded = eval("(" + responseText + ")");
        
        		//krijemo div ako nema rezultata
        		if (decoded.content === null || escape(typed_search_val.value) === "") {
        			document.getElementById('left_search_suggest').style.visibility="hidden"; //krijemo 'wait' div
    				setTimeout("document.getElementById('left_search_wait').style.visibility='hidden';", 100);
    				return;
        		} else {
        			document.getElementById('left_search_suggest').style.visibility="visible";
        		}
        
        		e = document.getElementById(decoded.div_id);
        		e.innerHTML = '';
        
        		var str = decoded.content.split(/\n/gi);
        
        		num_results = str.length - 1; // potrebno zbog fokusiranja poslednjeg reda u rezultatima kada se klikne na gore
        
        		for(i=0; i &lt; str.length - 1; i++) {
				//IE ne podrzava dinamicki dodeljene atribute... zato probamo sa javascriptom
				var suggest = '&lt;div onmouseover="javascript:left_suggestOver(this);" ';
				suggest += 'id="left_suggest_' + i + '" name="left_suggest_' + i + '" ';
				suggest += 'onmouseout="javascript:left_suggestOut(this);" ';
				suggest += 'onclick="javascript:left_setSearch(this.innerHTML);" ';
				suggest += 'class="left_suggest_link"&gt;' + str[i] + '&lt;/div&gt;';
				e.innerHTML += suggest;
			}
		
			//krijemo 'wait' div
	    		setTimeout("document.getElementById('left_search_wait').style.visibility='hidden';", 100);
		}
	}
	
	var opt = {
	   	// Use POST
	   	method: 'post',
	   	// Data
	   	data: $('left_search_form'),
	   	// Handle successful response
	   	onComplete: callback,
			
	   	evalScripts: true
	}
	
	var getData = function() {
		//prikazujemo 'wait' div
		document.getElementById('left_search_wait').style.visibility="visible";
		new Ajax('http://www.weather2umbrella.com/modules/mod_left_search/left_response.php', opt).request();
	}
	
	element = document.getElementById('left_search_keyword');
	if ( element.zid ) {
		clearTimeout(element.zid);
	}
	element.zid = setTimeout(getData ,500);
	
}
         </script>

           // World Map Mouseover Function
function update_map_mouseover(area, area_title) {
	el = document.getElementById('world_map_' + area);
	if (area &amp;&amp; el) {
		el.style.display = "block";
		if (area_title) Tip(area_title, BALLOON, true, ABOVE, true);
	}
}


// World Map Mouseout Function
function update_map_mouseout(area) {
	el = document.getElementById('world_map_' + area);
	if (area &amp;&amp; el) {
		el.style.display = "none";
		UnTip();
	}
}

         <script type="text/javascript">
          function changeSearchText(search_id) {
	el = document.getElementById(search_id);
	if (el.value == "Search") { 
		el.value = "Search"; 
	} 
	else 
	if (el.value == "Search") { 
		el.value = "Search"; 
	}

	if (el2 = document.getElementById('local_search_keyword')) {
		if (el2.value == "Search" || el2.value == "Search" ) {
			el2.value = "Search";
		}
		else
		if (el2.value == "Search" || el2.value == "Search" ) {
                        el2.value = "Search";
                }

	}

	if (el3 = document.getElementById('box_search_keyword')) {
		if (el3.value == "Search" || el3.value == "Search" ) {
			el3.value = "Search";
		}
		else
		if (el3.value == "Search" || el3.value == "Search" ) {
                        el3.value = "Search";
                }

	}


	timeout = setTimeout('changeSearchText(\'left_search_keyword\')', 500);
	
}

var timeout_counter;
timeout_counter = setTimeout('changeSearchText(\'left_search_keyword\')',500);

         <script type="text/javascript">
          function send_bug_report() {
	document.getElementById('bug_report_link').value = "%2F";
        var str = escape(document.getElementById('bug_message_text').value);
        if (str === "") {
                //alert('Unesite kratak opis!');
                //return;
        }

        var callback = function(responseText) {
                //alert(responseText);
                var decoded = eval("(" + responseText + ")");
                e = document.getElementById(decoded.div_id);
		tmp = e.innerHTML;
                e.innerHTML = 'Thank you for your help!'+'&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;';
		
                setTimeout("document.getElementById('bug_report_info').innerHTML='Have you noticed a BUG?&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;';", 3000);
        }

        var opt = {
                // Use POST
                method: 'post',
                // Data
                data: $('report_bug_form'),
                // Handle successful response
                onComplete: callback,
                evalScripts: true
        }

        new Ajax('http://www.weather2umbrella.com/modules/mod_w2u_city_weather_small/report_bug.php', opt).request();

}

function check_image_and_send_report() {
	//alert(document.getElementById('content_article_id').value+" "+document.getElementById('bug_report_check').value);
	if (document.getElementById('bug_report_check').value != document.getElementById('content_article_id').value.substr(5, 5)) alert('Failed text!'); 
	else {
		send_bug_report();
		showlayer('bugReport');
	}
}

function change_capatcha_image() {
	var random_n = (Math.round(Math.random()*10000)+10000);
	document.getElementById('check_image').src = 'http://www.weather2umbrella.com/check_image.php?check_image='+random_n;
	document.getElementById('content_article_id').value = '91732'+random_n+'42317';
	document.getElementById('bug_report_check').value = '';
	if (document.getElementById('bugReport').style.display == "block") document.getElementById('bug_report_check').focus();
}

             <script>
              function activate_weather(day, type, day_date) {
		for (n=0;n&lt;7;n++) { // krijemo sve layere sa ikonicama na mapi
			//document.getElementById('wea_'+n).style.backgroundImage = "url(/modules/mod_w2u_custom_city_icons_1/tmpl/images/"+type+"/module_background.jpg)";
			document.getElementById('wea_'+n).style.display = "none";
			document.getElementById('day_'+n).className = "inactive_day";
		}
		document.getElementById('wea_'+day).style.display = "block"; // un-hideujemo aktivni-dan layer sa ikonicama
		document.getElementById('day_'+day).className = "active_day"; // poplavljujemo aktivni dan
		document.getElementById("day_date").innerHTML = day_date; // ispis selektovanog datume
		document.getElementById('day').value=day; // datum za degree_model formu	
		document.map_click_form.day.value = day; // datum za klik na zemlju na mapi
		
		document.zoom_in_form.day.value = day; // datum za klik na zoom_in na mapi
		document.zoom_out_form.day.value = day; // datum za klik na zoom_in na mapi
		document.go_west_form.day.value = day; // datum za klik na zoom_in na mapi
		document.go_east_form.day.value = day; // datum za klik na zoom_in na mapi
		document.go_north_form.day.value = day; // datum za klik na zoom_in na mapi
		document.go_south_form.day.value = day; // datum za klik na zoom_in na mapi

	}

	function mapCountryClick(country, country_id, country_code, region) {
                        //alert(country+"-"+region+", "+document.map_click_form.day.value);
                        document.map_click_form.country_id.value = country_id;
                        document.map_click_form.country_code.value = country_code;
                        document.map_click_form.country.value = country;
                        document.map_click_form.region.value = region;
                        day = document.map_click_form.day.value;

			//W2U SEF			
			document.map_click_form.action = "en/weather-forecast-"+country.replace(/ /g, "-").toLowerCase()+"/"+"eta2/3/"+country_id+"/"+day;

                        document.map_click_form.submit();
        }
